942:) -> bool:\\n  > 943:    \\\"\\\"\\\"Write a preliminary result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE sentinel.\\n  > 944:\\n  > 945:    This function is a deterministic fallback ensuring If called after status determination,\\n  > 951:    the sentinel file will not affect the already-computed status.\\n  > 952:\\n  > 953:    **Concurrency**: Assumes single-threaded execution (one phase at a time). If the\\n  > 954:    sprint loop is parallelised in future, this function must be replaced with an\\n  > 955:    ``O_EXCL``-based atomic write to prevent TOCTOU races between the exists-check\\n  > 956:    and the write.\\n  > 957:\\n  > 958:    **Sentinel contract**: Writes ``EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\\\\\\\\n`` so that\\n  > 959:    ``_determine_phase_status()`` branch 3 (``result_file.exists()`` → CONTINUE check\\n  > 960:    at line 1024) returns ``PhaseStatus.PASS`` instead of falling through to the\\n  > 961:    ``PASS_NO_REPORT`` branch (line 1045). This sentinel is intentionally minimal;\\n  > 962:    the executor result file written by ``_write_executor_result_file()`` afterwards\\n  > 963:    will overwrite it with the authoritative structured report.\\n  > 964:\\n  > 965:    Args:\\n  > 966:        config: Sprint configuration providing ``result_file(phase)`` path.\\n  > 967:        phase: The phase whose result file to write.\\n  > 968:        started_at: Phase start time as a POSIX timestamp (``datetime.timestamp()``).\\n  > 969:            Used for the freshness guard: if a result file already exists with\\n  > 970:            ``st_mtime >= started_at`` and ``st_size > 0``, it is assumed to be a\\n  > 971:            valid agent-written file and is left untouched (no-op).\\n  > 972:\\n  > 973:    Returns:\\n  > 974:        ``True`` if the sentinel file was written, ``False`` if the file was preserved\\n  > 975:        (freshness guard triggered) or an ``OSError`` prevented the write. This is distinct from single-budget exhaustion.\n\n---\n\n## v2.26 Placeholder Behavior\n\n**Function:** `_print_terminal_halt()` (sprint executor layer)\n\nIn v2.26, `_print_terminal_halt()` does **not** distinguish between single-budget and dual-budget exhaustion. When the sprint halts due to budget exhaustion, the terminal output includes a generic halt message without specific dual-budget diagnostic information.\n\n**Current behavior (v2.26 placeholder):**\n- Turn budget exhausted → sprint halts, `_print_terminal_halt()` called with TURN_BUDGET_EXHAUSTED status\n- Token budget exhausted → sprint halts, `_print_terminal_halt()` called with TOKEN_BUDGET_EXHAUSTED status\n- Both exhausted → whichever triggers first wins; the other condition is not separately reported\n- No combined \"DUAL_EXHAUSTED\" diagnostic output exists\n\nThe placeholder behavior is: log whichever budget was exhausted first, halt cleanly, emit resume command. No special dual-exhaustion handling.\n\n---\n\n## v2.26 Deferral Scope\n\nThe following FR-077 behaviors are **deferred to v2.26+**:\n1. Detecting the dual-exhaustion condition (both budgets exhausted within the same sprint run)\n2. Emitting a distinct `DUAL_BUDGET_EXHAUSTED` status in the execution log\n3. Providing user-facing recommendations for dual-exhaustion (e.g., \"reduce task scope and increase both budgets\")\n4. Distinguishing dual-exhaustion in the result file (`EXIT_RECOMMENDATION` differentiation)\n\n---\n\n## Phase 4 T04.07 Implementation Note\n\nPhase 4 T04.07 will implement FR-077 dual-budget-exhaustion detection by:\n1. Checking both `TurnLedger.available` and token budget remaining after each step\n2. If both are ≤ 0 or below threshold simultaneously, set status `DUAL_BUDGET_EXHAUSTED`\n3. Modify `_print_terminal_halt()` to accept and render this new status with specific messaging\n4. Write `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT_DUAL_EXHAUSTED` (or similar) to result file\n\n**No Phase 2 or Phase 3 work is blocked by this deferral.**\n\n---\n\n## No Remaining Ambiguity\n\n- v2.26 behavior: placeholder (single-budget-wins logic)\n- v2.26 implementation target: T04.07 adds dual-exhaustion detection and distinct output\n- All downstream phases can proceed without dependency on FR-077 dual logic\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":9115,"cache_read_input_tokens":50545,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":9115,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":24,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3658f9d6-282a-4cf1-bbbb-e5f857c7acca","uuid":"75062696-7a92-4d11-840f-37563e2481f7"}
